        <div class="block block-system" id="block-system-main">
         <div class="content">
          <div class="node node-workout clearfix" id="node-46946">
           <div class="nodeHeader">
            <h1>
             40 Minute Blast - Abs, Cardio And Resistance Workout
            </h1>
            <div class="socialButtons">
             <div class="addthis_sharing_toolbox">
             </div>
            </div>
            <div class="nodeSummary">
             <div class="field field-name-field-summary field-type-text-long field-label-hidden">
              <div class="field-items">
               <div class="field-item even">
                A cardio, weights and abs workout perfect for those days when you need to do something fun at the gym. Simply grab a heavy and light set of dumbbells and go!
               </div>
              </div>
             </div>
            </div>
           </div>
           <!-- End Node Header -->
           <article class="nodeBody" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Article">
            <meta content="40 Minute Blast - Abs, Cardio And Resistance Workout" itemprop="name"/>
            <meta content="40 Minute Blast - Abs, Cardio And Resistance Workout" itemprop="headline"/>
            <meta content="A cardio, weights and abs workout perfect for those days when you need to do something fun at the gym. Simply grab a heavy and light set of dumbbells and go!" itemprop="description"/>
            <meta content="https://cdn.muscleandstrength.com/sites/default/files/field/image/workout/cardio-blast-450.jpg" itemprop="image"/>
            <meta content="John Gormen" itemprop="author"/>
            <meta content="Feb 2013" itemprop="datePublished"/>

             <div class="workoutSummary">
              <h2 class="blueStripe">
               Workout Summary
              </h2>
              <div class="data-wrap">
               <div class="data-row row">
                <label>
                 Main Goal
                </label>
                <div class="field field-name-field-main-goal field-type-list-text field-label-hidden">
                 <div class="field-items">
                  <div class="field-item even">
                   General Fitness
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
               <div class="data-row row">
                <label>
                 Workout Type
                </label>
                <div class="field field-name-field-workout-type field-type-list-text field-label-hidden">
                 <div class="field-items">
                  <div class="field-item even">
                   Cardio
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
               <div class="data-row row">
                <label>
                 Training Level
                </label>
                <div class="field field-name-field-experience-level field-type-list-text field-label-hidden">
                 <div class="field-items">
                  <div class="field-item even">
                   Beginner
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
               <div class="data-row row">
                <label>
                 Days Per Week
                </label>
                <div class="field field-name-field-days-per-week field-type-list-text field-label-hidden">
                 <div class="field-items">
                  <div class="field-item even">
                   1
                  </div>
                 </div>
                </div>
               </div>
               <div class="data-row row">
                <label>
                 Equipment Required
                </label>
                <div class="field-type-list-text">
                 Bodyweight, Dumbbells
                </div>
               </div>
               <div class="data-row row">
                <label>
                 Target Gender
                </label>
                Male &amp; Female
               </div>
               <div class="data-row row last">
                <label>
                 Author
                </label>
                <div class="field field-name-field-author field-type-node-reference field-label-hidden">
                 <div class="field-items">
                  <div class="field-item even">
                   <a href="/authors/john-gormen">
                    John Gormen

             <div class="row">
              <h2 class="blueStripe">
               Workout Description
              </h2>
              <div class="field field-name-body field-type-text-with-summary field-label-hidden">
               <div class="field-items">
                <div class="field-item even">
                 <p>
                  Strap on your game face, stretch, get warmed up and let's roll!
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  This is cardio and
                  <a href="/workouts/abs">
                   abs workout
                  </a>
                  that you can use to break the gym boredom. It also involves resistance training. If you are feeling like you need a break from the same old dull workout routine, but don't want to train like a wet noodle either, give this a try.
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  You will cycle between a resistance exercise, cardio and an abdomimal exercise. Rest 15-30 seconds between each step of the workout.
                 </p>
                 <p>
                  It is best to use 2 sets of
                  <a href="/exercises/dumbbell">
                   dumbbells
                  </a>
                  for this workout, a heavier set for the tougher lifts, and a lighter set for
                  <a href="/exercises/isolation">
                   isolation movements
                  </a>
                  . You can also set up near a dumbbell rack and grab dumbbells as you need them, if possible.
                 </p>
                 <table class="workoutTable">

               <div class="field field-name-comment-body field-type-text-long field-label-hidden">
                <div class="field-items">
                 <div class="field-item even">
                  <p>
                   Hello -- I had a chance to try out the routine, and to facilitate the logistics in my situation, I made the following changes:
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   I combined the treadmill routines into two five minute exercises, walking and then running, at the beginning of the workout. When I did the walking, I made sure to have the treadmill at the highest incline setting. By the time I completed the entire workout routine, I had worked up a sweat.
                  </p>
                  <p>
                   Does my making the above changes run counter to the goals set by the program?
                  </p>
